CREATE TABLE movies (id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY, title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, genre VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, release_date DATE);

CREATE TABLE directors (id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, age INT NOT NULL, gender VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL, nationality VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL);

CREATE TABLE actors (id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, age INT NOT NULL, gender VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL);</t><s>INSERT INTO directors (name, age, gender, nationality) VALUES ('Lana Wachowski', 56, 'Female', 'American') ON CONFLICT (name) DO UPDATE SET gender = EXCLUDED.gender, nationality = EXCLUDED.nationality;</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE awards (id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, category VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, year INT NOT NULL);

CREATE TABLE studios (id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, headquarters VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL);

CREATE TABLE movies (id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY, title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, genre VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, release_date DATE);

CREATE TABLE directors (id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, age INT NOT NULL, gender VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL, nationality VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL);

CREATE TABLE actors (id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL, age INT NOT NULL, gender VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL);</t><s>insert into directors (name, age, gender, nationality) values ('lana wachowski', 56, 'female', 'american') on conflict (name) do update set gender = excluded.gender, nationality = excluded.nationality;</s>
